# Plot Events

# Blackmail									7250-7270
# Drunken Plot Member						7040-7045

# Ultimatum event series					8000-8040
# Plot to kill character 					8220-8227

# Assassination notification events			8250-8299
#											7700-7999


###########################################
# Blackmail
###########################################
# 7250-7270

##########################################
#Buy loyalty plot (by knuckey)
namespace = plot_event

# The plot has been leaked
character_event = {
	id = 7250
	desc = "EVTDESC7250"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
			has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
			has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
			has_plot = plot_kidnap_character
			has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
			has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason
			has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
			has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
		}
		is_plot_active = no
		num_of_plot_backers = 1
		job_spymaster = {
			NOT = { is_plot_target_of = PREV }
		}
		top_liege = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				OR = { higher_tier_than = baron is_patrician = yes }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { any_backed_character = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { any_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_blackmailed } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { #CK2+
		months = 120
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_dumb_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = temperate
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}	
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7250"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			top_liege = {
				random_realm_lord = {
					limit = {
						OR = { higher_tier_than = baron is_patrician = yes }
					
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { any_backed_character = { character = ROOT } }
						NOT = { any_liege = { character = ROOT } }
						employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_blackmailed } }
					}
					letter_event = { id = 7255 days = 1 }
				}
			}	
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail or not
letter_event = {
	id = 7255
	desc = "EVTDESC7255"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7255"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
		}
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7260 days = 1 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7260" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7255"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail attempt
letter_event = {
	id = 7260
	desc = "EVTDESC7260"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7260"
		wealth = -100
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7265 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7260"
		set_character_flag = abort_plot
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}		
		plot_target_char = { #CK2+
			opinion = {
				modifier = scheming_bastard
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}					
			if = {
				limit = { 
					liege = { 
						NOT = { character = PREV } 
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = scheming_bastard
						months = 120
					}			
				}					
			}				
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7270 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail succeded
letter_event = {
	id = 7265
	desc = "EVTDESC7265"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		treasury = 100
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_blackmailed
			who = FROM
			months = 120
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail failed
letter_event = {
	id = 7270
	desc = "EVTDESC7270"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7270"
	}
}


###########################################
# Drunken Plot Member
###########################################
# 7040-7045

# Drunk plot member spills the beans
character_event = {
	id = 7040
	desc = "EVTDESC7040"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
				has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
				has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
				has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
				has_plot = plot_kidnap_character
				has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
				has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason
				has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
				has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
			}
			is_plot_active = no
			NOT = { has_character_flag = event7040 }
			NOT = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { #CK2+
		months = 1000

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_dumb_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = temperate
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7040"
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
					has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
					has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
					has_plot = plot_instigate_revolt
					has_plot = plot_kidnap_character
					has_plot = plot_kidnap_liege
					has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason
					has_plot = plot_fabricate_treason_liege
					has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = event7040 }
				NOT = {
					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = revealed_plot
				months = 120
			}
			set_character_flag = event7040
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7045 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7045
	desc = "EVTDESC7045"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7045"
		set_character_flag = abort_plot
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = scheming_bastard
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					liege = { NOT = { character = PREV } }
				}
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = devious_plotter
						months = 120
					}			
				}					
			}	
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - seniority
letter_event = {
	id = 8005
	desc = "EVTDESC8005"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_succ_seniority }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_seniority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { culture = summer_islander }
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = { 
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}	
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
							}	
						}
					}	
				}	
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_succ_seniority }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8076 }
			}
			liege = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8076 }
				}	
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8055 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_seniority
					letter_event = { id = 8075 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_succ_seniority = { # The target (title) of the faction
				succession = seniority
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								culture_group = andal
								culture_group = first_men
								culture = stone_dornish
							}
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								culture_group = iron_isles_culture
								culture = eastern_valyrian
								culture = mantaryan
								culture = tolosi
								culture = elyrian
							}
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = agnatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								culture = salt_dornish
								culture = sand_dornish
								culture = rhoynar
							}
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = true_cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							culture = lengi
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = enatic_cognatic
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8005"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				culture = summer_islander
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
					}	
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 2.0 } }
			}
			
			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8105 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_seniority
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Ultimatum - primogeniture
letter_event = {
	id = 8010
	desc = "EVTDESC8010"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_succ_primogeniture }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_primogeniture
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = andal
						culture_group = first_men
						culture_group = dornish
					}
				}	
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = { 
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}	
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
							}	
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_succ_primogeniture }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8081 }
			}
			liege = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8081 }
				}	
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8060 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_primogeniture
					letter_event = { id = 8080 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_succ_primogeniture = { # The target (title) of the faction
				succession = primogeniture
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								culture_group = andal
								culture_group = first_men
								culture = stone_dornish
							}
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								culture_group = iron_isles_culture
								culture = eastern_valyrian
								culture = mantaryan
								culture = tolosi
								culture = elyrian
							}
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = agnatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								culture = salt_dornish
								culture = sand_dornish
								culture = rhoynar
							}
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = true_cognatic
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = {
							culture = lengi
						}
					}	
					gender_succ = enatic_cognatic
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					culture_group = andal
					culture_group = first_men
					culture_group = dornish
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
					}	
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 2.0 } }
			}
			
			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8110 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_primogeniture
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_primogeniture power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14

			}
		}
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

				factor = 0

				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_feudal_elective power = 0.6 } } }

							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud

							}

						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8086 }

					letter_event = { id = 8085 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {

				succession = feudal_elective
				if = {

# Ultimatum - crown authority
letter_event = {
	id = 8025
	desc = "EVTDESC8025"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_lower_crown_authority }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = { 
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}	
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
							}	
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {	
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_lower_crown_authority }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8094 }
			}
			liege = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8094 }
				}	
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8067 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
					letter_event = { id = 8095 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_lower_crown_authority = { # The target (title) of the faction
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_1 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_0
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_2 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_3 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_2
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = centralization_4 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = centralization_3
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_lowered_crown_authority
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
					}	
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction =faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 2.0 } }
			}
			
			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8117 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - gain a vassal title
letter_event = {
	id = 8030
	desc = "EVTDESC8030"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8068 }
				any_plot_backer = {
					letter_event = { id = 8096 }
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			plot_target_title = {
				usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREV type = claim }
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9 #CK2+
				FROM = { plot_power = 1.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75 #CK2+
				FROM = { plot_power = 1.75 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5 #CK2+
				FROM = { plot_power = 2.0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Liege likes me
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value = 40
						}
						dynasty = ROOT
					}	
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8118 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
		}
	}
}

# Regent responds to crown authority ultimatum
letter_event = {
	id = 8026
	desc = "EVTDESC8026"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_lower_crown_authority }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				liege = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 33 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				liege = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 66 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				liege = { NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 99 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_lower_crown_authority power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							#strong loyalists
							AND = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
								any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
							}
						}
					}	
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = { 
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}	
							}
						}
						liege = {
							liege = {
								NOT = { character = PREV }
								OR = {
									opinion = { who = PREV value = 40 }
									dynasty = PREV
									is_married = PREV
									primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
								}	
							}
						}	
					}	
				}	
			}

# Ultimatum - Independence
letter_event = {
	id = 8035
	desc = "EVTDESC8035"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_independence }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_independence
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000" # Fold to demand
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_independence power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = { 
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}	
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
							}	
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_independence }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8093 }
			}
			liege = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8093 }
				}	
			}

				letter_event = { id = 8069 }

					faction = faction_independence
					letter_event = { id = 8097 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_independence
				set_defacto_liege = THIS
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
		
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_granted_independence
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {

					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_claimant power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Demand accepted - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8061
	desc = "EVTDESC8061"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		supported_claimant = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_very_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				who = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		supported_claimant = {
			hidden_tooltip = { #This stops wars to depose liege
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = installed_pretender
					duration = 10
					hidden = yes
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = yes
					host = { character = FROM  }
				}
				prisoner = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #If patrician enforcing claim on republic hold election in their favour
					is_patrician = yes
					FROM = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
					liege = { character = FROM }
					ROOT = { supported_claimant_title = { is_primary_holder_title = yes } }			
				}
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					prestige = 75000 
					FROM = { character_event = { id = REP.903 tooltip = TOOLTIPREP.903 } }
				}
				ROOT = { set_character_flag = patrician_usurp }		
			}
			ROOT = {
				supported_claimant_title = {
					# If the claimant has the wrong government type, take care of that first.
					if = {
						limit = {
							higher_tier_than = PREVPREV
							holder_scope = {
								OR = {
									is_tribal = yes
									is_feudal = yes
									is_nomadic = yes
								}	
							}
							ROOT = {
								NOT = { has_character_flag = patrician_usurp }	
								supported_claimant = {								
									is_ruler = yes
									OR = {
										is_theocracy = yes
										is_republic = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = { 
							supported_claimant = {
								hidden_tooltip = { #Universal on death/abdication event
									if = {
										limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
										set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
									}
									set_character_flag = abdication
									character_event = { id = 45341 } 
									clr_character_flag = abdication
									clr_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
								}
								abdicate = yes 
							} 
						}
					}
					if = { 	
						limit = {	
							holder_scope = { has_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars }
							#tier = KING
						}
						ROOT = { supported_claimant = { set_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars } }
					}
					if = { 	
						limit = {	
							holder_scope = { 
								OR = {
									has_character_flag = supporting_king 
									has_character_flag = neutral 
									has_character_flag = against_king 
									has_character_flag = rebel_leader
								}		
							}
							#tier = KING
						}
						ROOT = { supported_claimant = { set_character_flag = neutral } }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { NOT = { has_character_flag = patrician_usurp } } }
						usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded_and_vassals = { target = PREVPREV type = claim }
					}					
					hidden_tooltip = {
						if = {
							limit = { holder_scope = { has_character_flag = neutral } }
							holder_scope = { any_vassal = { set_character_flag = neutral } }
						}
						if = {
							limit = { title = e_iron_throne } #Lose crownlands
							holder_scope = { character_event = { id = maintenance.37 } } 
						}						
					}
				}
			}	
			character_event = { id = maintenance.26 } #Vanilla bug resets laws, so fix empire tracker law and primogeniture
			character_event = { id = maintenance.21 } #Take dejure vassals if King title usurped	
			ROOT = { clr_character_flag = patrician_usurp }	
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_close_relative = PREV
						NOT = { age = 16 }
					}
					move_character = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = rebel_leader
					e_iron_throne = {
						holder_scope = { NOT = { war_with = PREVPREV } }
					}
				}
				remove_trait = rebel_leader
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = regency.55 days = 2 } } #Become Regent if possible
	}
}

			limit = {
				controls_religion = no
				tier = ROOT
				NOT = { 
					dejure_liege_title = { 
						OR = {
							FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV } 
							dejure_liege_title = {
								OR = {
									FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV } 
									dejure_liege_title = { FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV } }
								}	
							}
						}	
					}	
				}
			}
			add_weak_pressed_claim = FROM
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			character_event = { id = mega_wars.50 } #Character wins indep war maintenance
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_independence_ultimatum_taken
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = "indep_faction_won"
				duration = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

# Demand rejected - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8111
	desc = "EVTDESC8100"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8100"
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				supported_claimant = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			faction_claimant = { # The target (title) of the faction
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = claim_on_liege
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					supported_claimant = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			if = { #If external ruler flag as such so top liege can intervene
				limit = {
					supported_claimant = {
						is_ruler = yes
						independent = no
						NOT = { any_liege = { character = FROM } }
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = external_claimant
			}	
			hidden_tooltip = {
				supported_claimant = {
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_supported_claimant
						years = 100
					}
				}
			}
			faction_claimant = { # The target (title) of the faction
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = other_claim_on_liege
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
		}
		
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies } }
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC8100"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8100"
		
		clr_character_flag = faction_lower_CA_ultimatum_taken
		
		faction_lower_crown_authority = { # The target (title) of the faction
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = lower_crown_authority_law
				faction = faction_lower_crown_authority
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies } }
	}
}

# Demand rejected - gain a vassal title
letter_event = {
	id = 8118
	desc = "EVTDESC8118"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8118"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		hidden_tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		plot_target_title = {
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = claim_on_vassal_plot
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8118"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -100
		any_plot_backer = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_coward
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				letter_event = { id = 8120 }
			}
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
	}
}

# Demand rejected - Independence
letter_event = {
	id = 8119
	desc = "EVTDESC8100"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8100"
		
		clr_character_flag = faction_independence_ultimatum_taken
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = "indep_war"
				duration = 100
			}
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_independence
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = "indep_war"
					duration = 100
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						FROM = { tier = EMPEROR }
					}
					set_character_flag = against_king
				}
			}
		}	
		war = {
			target = FROM
			casus_belli = cb_faction_independence
			faction = faction_independence
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies } }
	}
}

# Inform vassal - plot is abandoned
letter_event = {
	id = 8120
	desc = "EVTDESC8120"
	
	show_from_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_coward
				who = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8120"
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_coward
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisoned Wine
character_event = {
	id = 8150
	desc = "EVTDESC8150"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				has_opinion_modifier = { #Attending plotter's wedding
					modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
					who = ROOT
				}
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { #Hosting wedding
					modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
					who = ROOT
				}
				AND = { #Attending plotter's feast
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					ROOT = { has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast is_liege_of = ROOT }
				}
				AND = { #Hosting feast
					has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = guest_feast_started liege = { character = ROOT } }
				}
				AND = { #Attending the same wedding
					ROOT = {
						any_liege = {
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { 
								modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
								who = ROOT
							}
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { 
								modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
								who = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { #Attending the same feast
					has_character_flag = guest_feast_started
					liege = {
						has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast
						any_vassal = { character = ROOT }
					}
					ROOT = {
						has_character_flag = guest_feast_started		
					}
				}
			}	
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8150" # The conspirators provide the poison
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8150" # Buy the poison
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8150" # Buy the poison
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC8150" # Hemlock goes well with the Red...
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			learning = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - Plot backer requests funds
character_event = {
	id = 8152
	desc = "EVTDESC8152"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8152"
		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				from = ROOT
				to = FROM
				value = 1.0
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 8153 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8153" } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8152"
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 8154 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8154" } }
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - plot backer receives funds

# Poisoned Wine - plot backer does NOT receive funds

	id = 8154
	desc = "EVTDESC8154"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8154" # Pay for it myself
		scaled_wealth = -1.0

	}

		FROM = { clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8155
	desc = "EVTDESC8155"
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		prisoner = no
		
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = food_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = food_murder
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8155" # Drinks the wine
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

character_event = {
	id = 8156
	desc = "EVTDESC8156"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8156
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_poison
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_poison
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8158
	desc = "EVTDESC8158"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8158"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 8172 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8152" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8170" # Bribe a Guard
		trigger = {
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 8180 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC8170" # I know just the person for the job...
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			intrigue = 10
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
		}
		
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
			character_event = { id = 8180 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {

	id = 8176
	desc = "EVTDESC8176"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8176"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}	
}

# Falling Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8178
	desc = "EVTDESC8178"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8178"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

									FROM = {

										}
									}

							}
						}

						hidden_tooltip = {
							character_event = { id = 7515 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7515" }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {

				letter_event = { id = 7506 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7506" }
			}
		}
	}

				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }

					}

			}

		name = "EVTOPTB7505"

character_event = {

	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {

			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {

# Archer Ambush - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7705
	desc = "EVTDESC7705"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7705" # Hit by arrows
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {

				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }

					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

					}

						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14

						intrigue = 17

						factor = 1.33

					}

						factor = 1.33

						factor = 0.75

					}

						factor = 0.75

					character_event = { id = 7707 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7705" # Avoids arrows
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}

						factor = 0.75

# Archer Ambush - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7706
	desc = "EVTDESC7706"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7706"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Archer Ambush - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7708
	desc = "EVTDESC7708"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7708"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

### MANURE EXPLOSION
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Manure Explosion
character_event = {
	id = 7720
	desc = "EVTDESC7720"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7720" # The conspirators provide the manure
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7722 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7720" # Buy the manure
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7720" # Buy the manure
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7720" # Knows farmer
		tooltip_info = stewardship
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			stewardship = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = "EVTOPTA7726"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7728
	desc = "EVTDESC7728"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7728"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Infanticide - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7745
	desc = "EVTDESC7745"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
					NOT = { age = 5 }
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
						NOT = { age = 5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7745" # Smothered
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }

					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}

					character_event = { id = 7746 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}

				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		}

		if = {

				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider

					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {

				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes

						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}

# Infanticide - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7746
	desc = "EVTDESC7746"
	picture = GFX_evt_family
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7746"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Infanticide - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7748
	desc = "EVTDESC7748"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7748"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Infanticide - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7753
	desc = "EVTDESC7753"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}				
			}	
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
		}	
		tooltip = { add_trait = dishonorable1 }
	}
}

### PRISON BREAK - PRISONERS ONLY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Prison Break
character_event = {
	id = 7760
	desc = "EVTDESC7760"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			prisoner = yes
			OR = { #Can't try this twice
				NOT = { has_character_flag = tried_prison_break }
				had_character_flag = { flag = tried_prison_break days = 1500 }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7760" # The conspirators get the man inside
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7762 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7760" # Hire killer
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7772 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7760" # Hire killer
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7772 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7760" # Knows the man for the job
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7772 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}
