# Prison Break - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7765
	desc = "EVTDESC7765"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { 
		set_character_flag = tried_prison_break 
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7765" # Tries to escape
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7766 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7767 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7765" # Does not try to escape
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

					}
					character_event = { id = 7768 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {

					}
					character_event = { id = 7769 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}

# Prison Break - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7766
	desc = "EVTDESC7766"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7766"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Prison Break - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7768
	desc = "EVTDESC7768"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7768"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC7773"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}				
			}	
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
		}	
		tooltip = { add_trait = dishonorable1 }
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Bathtub Drowning
character_event = {
	id = 7780
	desc = "EVTDESC7780"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			trait = incapable
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200

				power = 0.10

			}
		}
		modifier = {

			{

		}
		modifier = {

			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7780" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7782 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7785 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7785" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7780" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7792 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7785 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7785" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7780" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7792 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7785 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7785" } }

		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}

character_event = {
	id = 7785
	desc = "EVTDESC7785"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	}

				limit = {

						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}

					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes

						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {

character_event = {
	id = 7786
	desc = "EVTDESC7786"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7786"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathtub Drowning - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7788
	desc = "EVTDESC7788"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7788"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

# Boating Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7805
	desc = "EVTDESC7805"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7805" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {

			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		if = {

				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}

					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {

						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }

# Boating Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7806
	desc = "EVTDESC7806"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7806"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_drowning
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Boating Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7808
	desc = "EVTDESC7808"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7808"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### POISONOUS SNAKE
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisonous Snake
character_event = {
	id = 7820
	desc = "EVTDESC7820"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers

	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {

			has_plot = plot_kill_character

		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }

			plotter = ROOT

		}

# Poisonous Snake - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7825
	desc = "EVTDESC7825"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7825" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7826 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7827 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7825" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {

# Poisonous Snake - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7826
	desc = "EVTDESC7826"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7826"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_snakes
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_snakes
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisonous Snake - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7828
	desc = "EVTDESC7828"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7828"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC7833"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}				
			}	
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
		}	
		tooltip = { add_trait = dishonorable1 }
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Balcony Plummet
character_event = {
	id = 7840
	desc = "EVTDESC7840"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {

				power = 0.10
			}

				plotter = ROOT

			}
		}
		
		modifier = {

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

			}
		}
		modifier = {

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7840" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7842 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7852 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}

# Balcony Plummet - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7845
	desc = "EVTDESC7845"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7845" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7846 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7847 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7845" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

# Balcony Plummet - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7846
	desc = "EVTDESC7846"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7846"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Balcony Plummet - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7848
	desc = "EVTDESC7848"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7848"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

				trait = honest
			}

		}

	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 7860
	desc = "EVTDESC7860"

	is_part_of_plot = yes

		}
		plot_target_char = {

			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no

			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }

character_event = {
	id = 7865
	desc = "EVTDESC7865"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}

					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7866"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_arrow
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hunting Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7868
	desc = "EVTDESC7868"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7868"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 7885
	desc = "EVTDESC7885"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = fighting_murder
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = fighting_murder
	}

			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}

						factor = 0.75

						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }

						intrigue = 8
					}

						factor = 1.33

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17

						factor = 1.33

					}

			}
		}
	}

				limit = {

						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider

					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}

		hidden_tooltip = {

# Disguised Highwaymen - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7886
	desc = "EVTDESC7886"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7886"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disguised Highwaymen - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7888
	desc = "EVTDESC7888"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7888"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### CARRIAGE ACCIDENT
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Carriage Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7900
	desc = "EVTDESC7900"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60

# Carriage Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7905
	desc = "EVTDESC7905"
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7905" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 2 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						FROM = { NOT = { intrigue = 5 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 11 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 14 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						FROM = { intrigue = 17 }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7906 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7907 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7905" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
				kingsguard = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPBODYGUARDMURDERRESCUE }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						NOT = { intrigue = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {

						NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33
						intrigue = 17
					}
					modifier = {

# Carriage Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7906
	desc = "EVTDESC7906"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7906"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_fall
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Carriage Accident - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7908
	desc = "EVTDESC7908"
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7908"
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC7913"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}				
			}	
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
		}	
		tooltip = { add_trait = dishonorable1 }
	}
}

# Ultimatum - increase council power
letter_event = {
	id = 8215
	desc = EVTDESC8215
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_increase_council_power }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_increase_council_power
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 1 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 1 } }
					}	
				}	
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_increase_council_power }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8217 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8218 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_increase_council_power
					letter_event = { id = 8216 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_increased_council_power
				who = ROOT
				months = 12
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_increase_council_power = { # The target (title) of the faction
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = law_voting_power_1 }
					if = {
						limit = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = titles_voting_power_1 }
							if = {
								limit = { has_law = justice_voting_power_0 }
								add_law_w_cooldown = justice_voting_power_1
								break = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = titles_voting_power_0 }
							add_law_w_cooldown = titles_voting_power_1
							break = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_0 }
						add_law_w_cooldown = diplomacy_voting_power_1
						break = yes
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = law_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = law_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}			
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider
					trait = brave
					trait = ambitious
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = dragon_rider
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4 #Can request aid from liege
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT
						primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
					}	
				}
			}
			# Account for relative faction power
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.5 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 2.0 } }
			}
			
			#Traits
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.66
				trait = content
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8219 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_increase_council_power
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_increase_council_power power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# He will give loyalty for cash
letter_event = {
	id = plot_event.2
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.2"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_plot = plot_buy_loyalty
		plot_target_char = { character = FROM }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.2"  #fine give him what he wants!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 1 }
			}
		}	
		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = FROM
				value = 0.75
			}
		}	
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought
			who = FROM
			years = 100
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { 
				set_character_flag = loyalty_bought 
				letter_event = { id = plot_event.11 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					ai = yes
				}
				character_event = { id = plot_event.14  days = 75 }  #ai decides whether to try and improve realtions with target's liege
			}	
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.2"  #he asks too much
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}	
		set_character_flag = buy_loyalty_ploy_fail
		hidden_tooltip = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_bribe_rejected
				who = FROM
				years = 5
			}
			FROM = { 
				letter_event = { id = plot_event.12 days = 5 }

			}
		}	
		tooltip = {

				to = FROM
				value = 0.35
			}

		}

		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.3"  #keep trying to convince him

			factor = 15
		}

							has_job_title = job_spymaster

					}	
				}
			}

		}

			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					liege = {
						NOT = {
							any_courtier = {
								has_job_title = job_spymaster
							}
						}
					}

			}

		}

			}
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {

				years = 5
			}

	trigger = {

			FROM = {
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought }
				liege = { 
					ai = yes 
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_impressed_loyalty }
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_mildly_impressed_loyalty }
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_unimpressed_loyalty }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {  #try it
		name = "Try It"  
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		FROM = {
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.16  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.16" }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option= {  #not worth it
		name = "Not worth it"  
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		FROM = {
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.25  days = 5  }
			}
		}
	}
}
#Assign bought councillor mission (from interaction_events)
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.15
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.15"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	trigger = {
		event_target:bought_councillor = {
			has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought }
			character = FROM
		}	
	}
	
	option = {  #improve relations with their liege
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.15"  
		trigger = {
			event_target:bought_councillor = {
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought }
				character = FROM
				liege = { 
					ai = yes 
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_impressed_loyalty }
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_mildly_impressed_loyalty }
							has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_unimpressed_loyalty }
						}
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		event_target:bought_councillor = {
			character_event = { id = plot_event.16  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.16" }
			liege = {
				tooltip = { }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {  #sabotage job action
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.15"  
		trigger = {
			event_target:bought_councillor = {
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } 
				character = FROM
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_improve_relations
					has_job_action = action_fabricate_claims
					has_job_action = action_sow_dissent
					has_job_action = action_squeeze_peasants
					has_job_action = action_oversee_construction
					# AND = {
						# has_job_action = action_advance_eco_tech
						# liege = { ai = yes }
					# }	
					has_job_action = action_uncover_plots
					has_job_action = action_study_technology
					has_job_action = action_advance_mil_tech
					has_job_action = action_train_troops
					has_job_title = job_spiritual
					has_job_action = action_oversee_province
					has_job_action = action_pacify_province
				} 
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = job_action_sabotage }
					had_character_flag = {
						flag = job_action_sabotage
						days = 1825
					}	
				}	
			}	
		}
		event_target:bought_councillor = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_improve_relations }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32a" }
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_fabricate_claims }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32b" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_sow_dissent }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32c" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						has_job_action = action_squeeze_peasants 
						has_job_action = action_oversee_province
						has_job_action = action_pacify_province
					}	
				}
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32d" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_oversee_construction }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32e" }
			}
			# if = {
				# limit = { has_job_action = action_advance_eco_tech }
				# character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32e" }
			# }
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_uncover_plots }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32f" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_study_technology }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32g" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_organize_spies }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32h" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_advance_mil_tech }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32i" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_action = action_train_troops }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32j" }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }
				character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32k" }
			}
			# if = { # Dupiclate, tooltip combined with previous
				# limit = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }
				# character_event = { id = plot_event.32  days = 5  tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.32l" }
			# }
			liege = {
				tooltip = {
				}
			}
		}

	}

#bought character has second thoughts and decides what to do
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.27
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.27"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = loyalty_bought
	
	trigger = {
		
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = craven
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.27"  #ask for more money
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = greedy
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } 
			}
		}
		random_opinion_modifier_target = {
			limit = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } }
			letter_event = { id = plot_event.28 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.28" days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.27"  #sever relations
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } 
			}
		}
		random_opinion_modifier_target = {
			limit = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } }
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_betrayed_loyalty
				who = ROOT
				months = 60
			}
			letter_event = { id = plot_event.29 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.18" days = 3 }
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTDplot_event.27"  #I am happy
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } 
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCplot_event.27"  #they appear to be dead
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_opinion_modifier_target = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought } 
				}
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = loyalty_bought	
	}
}

#Bought character is asked to sabotage their job action
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.32
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.32"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	
	trigger = {
		has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_loyalty_bought }
	}
	
	option = {  #will do
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.16"  
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = plot_event.33 days = 3 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_action = action_improve_relations
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			location = {
				random_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						is_priest = no
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 20110 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20110" }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_action = action_fabricate_claims
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			location = {
				county = {
					holder_scope = {
						hidden_tooltip = {
							reverse_opinion = {
								who = ROOT
								modifier = opinion_fabricate_claims_bribe
								years = 5
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_action = action_sow_dissent
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			location = {
				random_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
						independent = no
					}
					character_event = { id = 20170 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20170" }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_squeeze_peasants
					has_job_action = action_oversee_province
					has_job_action = action_pacify_province
				}	
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			location = {
				# Inform barons about the rebels
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_liege_of = ROOT
						}
						set_character_flag = liege_informed
					}
				}
				any_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = liege_informed }
						ai = no
					}
					character_event = { id = 20215 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20215" }
				}
				# Inform liege
				ROOT = {
					liege = { letter_event = { id = 20216 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20216" } }
					clr_character_flag = liege_informed
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_oversee_construction
					#has_job_action = action_advance_eco_tech
				}	
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 20242 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20242a" } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_job_action = action_uncover_plots
					has_job_action = action_organize_spies
					has_job_action = action_advance_mil_tech
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_action = action_study_technology
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			location = {
				random_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = 20330 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20330a" }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_action = action_train_troops
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			location = {
				random_province_lord = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
						independent = no
					}
					character_event = { id = 20420 days = 100 random = 50 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP20420a" }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_title = job_spiritual
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			liege = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						age = 6
						NOT = { age = 16 }
						OR = {
							character = PREV
							AND = {
								same_liege = ROOT	
								is_close_relative = PREV
							}	
						}		
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { trait = dragon }		
					}
					random_list = {
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_intrigue }
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_stewardship }
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_diplomacy  }
						25 = { set_character_flag = maester_learning  }
					}
					if = { limit = { NOT = { personality_traits = 5 } }
						random_list = {
							75 = { }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_slothful }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_wroth  }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_proud  }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_arbitrary  }
							5 = { set_character_flag = maester_gluttonous  }
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = maester.19 }
				}			
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_job_title = job_spiritual
			}
			set_character_flag = job_action_sabotage
			liege = {
				remove_character_modifier = troops_likes_maester 
				character_event = { id = maester.36 days = 100 random = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {  #no
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.16"

#iKigndoms are revoked until less than 3 are held
character_event = { 
	id = plot_event.349
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { num_of_king_titles = 3 }
			random_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = KING
					can_be_given_away = yes
					is_primary_holder_title = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holder_scope = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } } }
					usurp_title = FROMFROM
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = kingdom_found }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						ROOT = { NOT = { has_character_flag = kingdom_found } }
						holder_scope = { character = FROMFROM } 
					}
					usurp_title = FROM
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = kingdom_found }
				}							
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_character_flag = kingdom_found 
					num_of_king_titles = 3
				}	
				clr_character_flag = kingdom_found 
				repeat_event = { id = plot_event.349 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

	war = no

		independent = no
		is_nomadic = no
		NOT = { government = military_command_government }
		tier = DUKE
		NOT = { trait = maester }
		NOT = { trait = archmaester }
		NOT = { trait = kingsguard }
		NOT = { trait = nightswatch }
		NOT = { trait = septon }
		NOT = { trait = drowned }
		NOT = { trait = red_priest }
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		liege = {
			tier = EMPEROR

				any_vassal = { tier = KING }
				num_of_king_titles = 2
			}
		}
		primary_title = {
			dejure_liege_title = {
				NOT = { any_war = { always = yes } } #is not being contested
				OR = { #is either vacant or held by liege
					has_holder = no 
					holder_scope = {
						is_liege_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = { #Cannot ask for primary LP title
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = non_iron_throne_westeros }

					}	
					NOT = {
						holder_scope = {
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = count
								location = { is_capital = yes }
								de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}	
				}

					NOT = { title = k_crownlands }
					has_holder = yes
				}

							title = k_sarnor
							title = k_north_valyria
						}

				}
				OR = { #Can only request Andalos or Rhoyne if correct culture
					NOT = { title = k_rhoynar }
					ROOT = { culture_group = dornish }
				}

							title = k_north

						}

							title = k_riverlands
							e_riverlands = { has_holder = yes }
						}

							e_vale = { has_holder = yes }
						}

							title = k_westerlands
							e_westerlands = { has_holder = yes }
						}

						}

							e_stormlands = { has_holder = yes }
						}

							e_dorne = { has_holder = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							title = k_iron_isles
							e_iron_isles = { has_holder = yes }
						}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = requested_lord_paramountcy }

	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_depose_liege
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
		if = { #disallow raising of levies whilst demand is considered
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = mega_war_no_levies
				duration = 14
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_depose_liege power = 0.6 } } }
					AND = {
						FROM = { NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_depose_liege power = 1.5 } } }
						OR = {
							trait = dragon_rider
							trait = brave
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
						}
					}
					#strong loyalists
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_crown_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						any_vassal = { faction_power = { faction = faction_liege_loyalist power = 0.75 } }
					}
					#Can request aid from liege
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							crownlaw_title = { 
								NOR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}	
							}
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_married = ROOT
								primary_title = { has_law = diplomacy_voting_power_1 } #The council votes
							}	
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_depose_liege }
				}
				letter_event = { id = plot_event.45 }
			}
			liege = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					letter_event = { id = plot_event.45 }
				}	
			}
			FROM = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_depose_liege
					letter_event = { id = plot_event.44 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				letter_event = { id = plot_event.43 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -15 }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_character_modifier = mega_war_no_levies }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_depose_liege power = 1.5 } }
				OR = {
					trait = craven
					trait = content
				}
				NOR = {
					trait = dragon_rider

# Demand accepted - Depose Liege
letter_event = {
	id = plot_event.43
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.43"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			current_heir = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_very_grateful
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
				reverse_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
					who = ROOT
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_depose_liege_ultimatum_taken
		FROM = {
			if = { #Triarch for life, revert to default law
				limit = { 
					primary_title = { has_law = republic_triarch_for_life } 
					ROOT = { NOT = { has_character_flag = title_triarch_for_life } }
				}
				family_palace = {
					current_heir = {
						if = { 
							limit = {
								has_character_flag = title_triarch_for_life
							}
							clr_character_flag = title_triarch_for_life
							remove_title = title_triarch_for_life
						}
					}				
				}	
				primary_title = { add_law = republic_law_0 }	
			}
			if = { #Night's watch versus Night's king, dethrone
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { trait = nightswatch }
					has_landed_title = k_nightswatch 
				}
				set_character_flag = destroy_nights_king
				tooltip = { k_nightswatch = { destroy_landed_title = THIS } }
			}
			current_heir = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						prisoner = yes
						host = { character = FROM  }
					}
					prisoner = no
				}
				save_event_target_as = deposed_heir
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = no } 
				hidden_tooltip = { #Universal on death/abdication event
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
						set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					}
					set_character_flag = abdication
					character_event = { id = 45341 } 
					clr_character_flag = abdication
					#clr_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					transfer_wealth_to_heir_effect = yes
				}
				abdicate = yes		
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
				character_event = { id = REP.903 tooltip = TOOLTIPREP.903B } #Hold Election
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no 
					liege = { NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT } }
				}
				event_target:deposed_heir = { reverse_banish = PREV }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = deposed_AGOT
				duration = 3650
			}
		}	
		hidden_tooltip = { #make sure kingdom is transferred in merchant republic
			top_liege = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						is_merchant_republic = yes
						tier = EMPEROR 
					}
					capital_scope = {
						kingdom = {
							if = {
								limit = { holder = FROM }
								gain_title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - BODYGUARD 
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.50
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.50"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			is_ruler = yes		
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_liege_of = ROOT					
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
							has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
							trait = kingsguard
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_landed_title = d_kingsguard }
				}	
				AND = {
					has_landed_title = e_iron_throne
					ROOT = { trait = kingsguard }
				}
			}
			prisoner = no
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}

		}

		}
		modifier = {

			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			plot_target_char = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.50" # The conspirator has plot power
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.61 days = 1 }
			}
		}	
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.50" # Bribes
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { martial = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.61 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.50" # Bribes
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { martial = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5

			}

		}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.54 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.54" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}

					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.50" # The conspirator has plot power
		trigger = {
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
			character_event = { id = plot_event.59 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8151" # Ask the Plotter for funds
		trigger = {
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = plot_event.750 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8152" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.50" # Hire archers
		trigger = {
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = plot_event.59 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCplot_event.50" # Knows when to strike
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			intrigue = 10
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
		}
		
		random_backed_character = {

			}
			character_event = { id = plot_event.59 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion

	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this

character_event = {

	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.54"
	picture = "GFX_evt_shadow"
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {

					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}

				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

			}
		}
