# BODYGUARD  - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.55
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.55"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		kingsguard = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}		
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				move_character = ROOT
				remove_trait = kingsguard
			}	
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bodyguard }
				remove_title = title_bodyguard
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bloodrider }
				remove_title = title_bloodrider
			}			
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.55"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}	
}

# BODYGUARD  - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.57
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.57"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROMFROM } }
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}		
		}
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reveal_plot = yes 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.57"
		kingsguard = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
			}		
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				move_character = ROOT
				remove_trait = kingsguard
			}	
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					character = FROM
					character = FROMFROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bodyguard }
				remove_title = title_bodyguard
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_bloodrider }
				remove_title = title_bloodrider
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = trusting }
				NOT = { trait = paranoid }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38275 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = trusting }
			remove_trait = trusting
		}	
		if = { #Ai try to imprison plotter?
			limit = { 
				is_ruler = yes				
				ai = yes			
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROMFROM }
				FROMFROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
				break = yes
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_vassal_or_below = FROMFROM }
				FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = imprison_target }
				character_event = { id = imprisoned.1 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### PEACE BANNER ATTACK
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Peace Banner Attack
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.66
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.66"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	only_playable = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		war = yes
		plot_target_char = {
			is_ruler = yes
			war = yes
			any_current_enemy = { character = ROOT }
			age = 16
			NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			in_command = yes
			OR = { #Must be losing in the war
				any_war = {
					attacker = { character = ROOT }	
					defender = { character = PREVPREV }					
					NOT = { war_score = -50 }
				}
				any_war = {
					defender = { character = ROOT }	
					attacker = { character = PREVPREV }						
					war_score = 50
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
		NOT = { trait = honorable }
		NOT = { trait = honest }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power = 0.55
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			plot_power = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			plot_power = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			plot_power = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.66" # Do it
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				plot_target_char = {
					OR = {
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = { trait = ruthless }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = ruthless
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = cruel
			}			
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = plot_event.70 days = 1 }
			}
		}		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = plot_event.67 days = 15 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPplot_event.67" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.66" # Not this way
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = kind
			}			
		}
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.67
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.67"
	picture = GFX_evt_courier
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
			is_ruler = yes
			war = yes
		}
		is_ruler = yes
		war = yes
		any_current_enemy = { character = FROM }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		murder_success_calulator_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.67" # Killed
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_success
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_success
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = plot_event.68 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered		
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBplot_event.67" # Not killed
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = murder_fail
		}
		clr_character_flag = murder_fail
		hidden_tooltip = {		
			character_event = { id = plot_event.69 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
		}
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.68
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.68"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.68"
		plot_murder_discovered_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = yes }
			random_courtier = {	
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
				}	
				tooltip = { death = yes }
				save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard			
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
			kingsguard = {	
				limit = {
					is_alive = yes
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
				}	
				tooltip = { death = yes }
				save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				ai = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT }
			}
			tooltip = { death = yes }
			save_event_target_as = slayed_courtier
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.71 } } }
		death = {
			death_reason = death_murder_slayed
			killer = FROMFROM
		}
	}	
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Lives, murderer discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.69
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.69"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 11 } } # Consequences of discovery
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		FROMFROM = { 
			reveal_plot = yes 	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.69"
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_councillor = yes
				ai = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT }
			}
			tooltip = { death = yes }
			save_event_target_as = slayed_courtier	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = yes }
			random_courtier = {	
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_minor_title = title_bloodrider
						has_minor_title = title_bodyguard
					}
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
				}	
				random_list = {
					20 = { }
					20 = { add_trait = wounded }
					20 = { add_trait = maimed }
					20 = { 
						tooltip = { death = yes }
						save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard	
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = e_iron_throne }
			kingsguard = {	
				limit = {
					is_alive = yes
					in_command = no
					is_abroad = no
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROMFROM }
				}	
				random_list = {
					20 = { }
					20 = { add_trait = wounded }
					20 = { add_trait = maimed }
					20 = { 
						tooltip = { death = yes }
						save_event_target_as = slayed_bodyguard	
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = plot_event.72 } } }
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.71
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.71"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no 
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					OR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						same_realm = FROM
						primary_title = {
							OR = {
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
								FROM = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = plot_event.73 }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		FROM = {
			tooltip = {
				death = { 
					death_reason = death_murder_slayed
					killer = ROOT
				}
			}	
		}
		event_target:slayed_bodyguard = {
			death = { 
				death_reason = death_murder_slayed
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
		event_target:slayed_courtier = {
			death = { 
				death_reason = death_murder_slayed
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}		
		piety = -200
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = deceitful }
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = deceitful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38255 #Notify Deceitful
					}
				}				
			}	
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
		}	
		tooltip = { add_trait = dishonorable1 }
	}
}

# Peace Banner Attack - Notification: Failure, and discovered
character_event = {
	id = plot_event.72
	desc = "EVTDESCplot_event.72"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no 
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					OR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						same_realm = FROM
						primary_title = {
							OR = {
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
								FROM = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = plot_event.74 }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAplot_event.72"
		event_target:slayed_bodyguard = {
			death = { 
				death_reason = death_murder_slayed
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
		event_target:slayed_courtier = {
			death = { 
				death_reason = death_murder_slayed
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion
			tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		}
		piety = -100
		tooltip = { add_trait = dishonorable1 }
	}
}
